I just had to pay S&amp;H which was something like $2.75 for me. I&#x27;ve been using it about a week and a half and there&#x27;s plenty to last a few more weeks (I apply it once, daily).&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;So let me start by explaining my type of lashes and what I look for in a mascara. I have long, straight lashes that are of standard thickness (if I can say such a thing. Basically, they&#x27;re not thick but they&#x27;re not thin... just normal). And since my lashes are already long, when looking for a mascara I focus on volume and a nice consistency that is not too wet. I find wet mascaras tend to make more of a mess when applying and I can&#x27;t stand having to clean up around my eyes after applying; so, I suppose I like a thick, sturdy formula-- non-runny. Also, so far I don&#x27;t believe any mascara has the true ability to curl lashes--at least mine, so that value is never a focus. Eyelash curler is the only sure way I&#x27;ll get any curl.  SO, basically what I look for in a mascara is its capacity to add volume to my lashes and not make a mess! And this mascara has proven a winner!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To illustrate it&#x27;s ultimate test, I applied a regular amount one early morning as I was preparing to spend the day snowboarding. Now granted I was wearing goggles, there were plenty of times I had the goggles lifted off my face and was subject to the wintery conditions of the slopes. About half-way through the day or so I stopped to have lunch and while in the restroom inspecting my makeup, I noticed the mascara had not smeared, smudged, or flaked. Any definition they may have had from my curler was done seeing as how facial steam in my goggles straightened them but the volume on the lashes themselves was as they were when first applied. By the end of the day I was extremely exhausted, realized my car was stuckin some snow, realized further that tow trucks were not willing to truck out to my location to help me, cried several tears in overwhelming exhaustion and frustration, and when I went to clean up my face in the restroom, was at least satisfied that my mascara did not run down my face or smear, but simply sat in small clumps under my eyes similar to how a tubing mascara comes off, and I very easily wiped it away with a tissue, still not smearing or smudging. I very much like a mascara that can hold up to watery eyes and a few tears and this did it. And considering it came off in a tasteful manner when I was really crying and rubbing my eyes, this passed the test.  (and btw, I did manage to get a tow truck to come out. But they had to come from over an hour away and it cost $300!!! Crazy. Ugh.).&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;So all in all, thumbs up for this mascara. It adds a tasteful amount of volume, layer-able for more if you&#x27;re headed for a night out, stays put, and doesn&#x27;t make a mess!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The reason I gave it 4 stars is because I think $20 is a little high and like I said, the volume is tasteful and buildable, but I wouldn&#x27;t say it added some crazy amount of volume-----BUT, considering all I went through with it, I&#x27;ll probably pay it for the full tube when my sample runs out ;)</li>
